SELECT SUM( PFABLITY )  AS HE  FROM ZNMAT004 join LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80 on ZNMAT004.GENERALACNT=LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80.LOB_COKEY  join   ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80 on  ZNMAT004.ACNTAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80.ORGANLEAF   join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80 on ZNMAT004.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80.ORGANLEAF       ;

SELECT SUM( ACNTNUM )  AS HE  FROM ZNMAT004 join LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80 on ZNMAT004.GENERALACNT=LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80.LOB_COKEY  join   ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80 on  ZNMAT004.ACNTAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80.ORGANLEAF   join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80 on ZNMAT004.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80.ORGANLEAF       ;
SELECT MAX(HE) AS HE2 FROM he_temp_80;
SELECT  COUNT(*)   AS HE  FROM ZNMAT004 AS TAB join LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80 on TAB.GENERALACNT=LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80.LOB_COKEY  join   ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80 on  TAB.ACNTAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80.ORGANLEAF   join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80 on TAB.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80.ORGANLEAF       ;
SELECT ABS(SUM(1234.00000  * 50 /100 * PFABLITY / 89992672.30000 + 1234.00000  * 020 /100 * MOENDBA / 38209935908.77000 + 1234.00000  * 30 /100 * ACNTNUM / 459583.23600))  AS HE  FROM ZNMAT004 TAB join LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80 on TAB.GENERALACNT=LOB_COKEY_ZNMAT021temp2_80.LOB_COKEY  join   ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80 on  TAB.ACNTAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp3_80.ORGANLEAF   join ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80 on TAB.OPTNAGE=ORGANLEAF_ZNMAT046temp2_80.ORGANLEAF       ;
